         <p>
          Im sure you know the value of building relationships with like-minded entrepreneurs online and gettingto know these folks by reading andcommentingon the content on their sites.
         </p>
         <p>
          The other day I was reading
          <a href="http://www.trafficgenerationcafe.com/10-ways-to-successfully-engage-influencers/" onclick="_gaq.push(['_trackEvent', 'outbound-article', 'http://www.trafficgenerationcafe.com/10-ways-to-successfully-engage-influencers/', 'Traffic Generation Caf']);" target="_blank">
           Traffic Generation Caf
          </a>
          written by a really cool lady,
          <em>
           Ana Hoffman
          </em>
          ,and was enjoying it very much, so decided to comment.I was so frustrated because much of my time was wasted. Why? Ineglected tofollow one ofmy own rules! I madethis new video tutorial to helpyou
          <strong>
           avoid my mistakes
          </strong>
          .
          <em>
           Plus I share two secrets of how I get so much done
          </em>
          .
         </p>

         <h2 style="text-align: center;">
          How to Save Time Commenting Online
          <br class=" sb-br"/>
          (and Keep Your Sanity)
         </h2>
         <p>
          Today Ill beteaching how to save time when commenting online (and keep your sanity). This is Carol Amato from CarolAmato.com.
         </p>
         <p>
          Well, surely by now you know that web sites which have visitor engagement, evidenced by comments about the content, are considered to be more valuable by search engines than sites with no engagement and zero comments.
         </p>
         <p>
          Providing value, building relationships and helping people by way of putting out relevant content has many rewards.
         </p>
         <p>
          Lets learn to comment smarter and faster, and protect our comments along the way so its a much more pleasant experience for you.
         </p>
         <p>
          There are many
          <em>
           blog commenting
          </em>
          software tools used today, and youre going to face a multitude of systems and platforms  so just be aware that there is a learning curve in understanding how to leave a comment on each of these.
         </p>
         <p>
          There is a trend seen in the industry leaders to shift toward commenting systems that allow social sharing of the comment with a link back to the content, and email notifications of follow-up comments, which land in the commenters Inbox, which of course, results in more traffic for you.
         </p>
         <p>
          I think you should use a comment plugin, system or software that integrates comments with social media, and this is becoming the new standard by the way.
         </p>
         <p>
          <strong>
           How to Comment Smarter and Faster
          </strong>
         </p>
         <p>
          People ask me all the time how Im able to get so much done, and Im going to reveal my secrets with you Before I built my online business, I worked in the medical field as a transcriptionist.
         </p>
         <p style="text-align: justify;">
          <img alt="text expander software" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-155907" height="285" src="http://cdn.carolamato.com/wp-content/uploads/2014/08/text-expander-software.png" width="500"/>
         </p>
         <p>
          Each day I logged into platforms based on software systems which detected each and every keystroke I made. I was drilled on the importance of minimizing my keystrokes for increased productivity and improved time efficiency. I was given access to powerful software which helped me in this area, and they were called text expanders.
         </p>
         <p>
          For example I could type three or four letters (or keystrokes) and have several large paragraphs replace these few letters.
         </p>
         <p>
          I used sticky notes around my computer monitor until I was adding several new short cuts per day. I then would take the sticky notes I knew off, and add others until I was able to save a lot of time.
         </p>
         <p style="text-align: justify;">
          Let me demonstrate how this works. Here I am with a little Notepad open. Something that I type over and over again is my email address so I created a shortcut. So iem and then x to execute and out pops:
          <span style="font-family: arial, helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: 12pt;">
           <img alt="Emal Address" class="aligncenter wp-image-159498 size-full" height="50" src="http://carolamatocdn.carolamato.netdna-cdn.com/wp-content/uploads/2014/08/emailaddresspic.jpg" width="300"/>
          </span>
         </p>
         <p>
          How many keystrokes would you rather type  the entire e-mail address or three or four? How many times have you typed your full address? I made a short cut for fu  full, ad  address, x to execute. Would you rather type four keystrokes, five keystrokes or this entire thing?
         </p>
         <p>
          How about phrases and sentences you use on a regular basis? hagd, x to execute = Have a great day. tc, x and out pops these two lines  Take Care,- Carol :)
         </p>
         <p>
          Its just phenomenal and very very powerful. So for the PC you want to check out some free software called
          <a href="http://carolsentme.com/shortkeys" onclick="_gaq.push(['_trackEvent', 'outbound-article', 'http://carolsentme.com/shortkeys', 'ShortKeys Lite']);" target="_blank">
           ShortKeys Lite
          </a>
          , and you can go to this web address right here.
         </p>
         <p>
          You can get up to 15 short keys for free, and then they have a paid version. But even if you just use the 15 short keys for your name, and your phone number and your Address and your email address, and maybe the URL to your website  it would really save you some time. And thats for folks that have a PC.
         </p>
         <p style="text-align: justify;">
          <a href="http://twitter.com/home/?status=Increase%20your%20reach%20-%20explode%20your%20blog%20commenting%20through%20the%20roof!%20via%20@Carol_Amato_%20http://carolsentme.com/save-time-commenting-online" onclick="_gaq.push(['_trackEvent', 'outbound-article', 'http://twitter.com/home/?status=Increase%20your%20reach%20-%20explode%20your%20blog%20commenting%20through%20the%20roof!%20via%20@Carol_Amato_%20http://carolsentme.com/save-time-commenting-online', '']);" target="_blank">
           <img alt="Click to tweet How to Save Time Commenting Online (and Keep Your Sanity)" class="aligncenter wp-image-155829 size-full" height="48" src="http://carolamatocdn.carolamato.netdna-cdn.com/wp-content/uploads/2014/07/tweet-carol-amato.jpg" width="538"/>
          </a>
         </p>
         <p>
          Folks on a Mac can download TypeIt4Me, which I have and its phenomenal. Theres a free trial but then its a paid program.
         </p>
         <p>
          You can search for text expander for free on Google and see if there are any free programs.
         </p>
         <p>
          Just think about how using text expanders or short keys could revolutionize your blog commenting (and social media engagement) and any typing task you have to do!Its a solution thats free or very inexpensive.
         </p>
         <p>
          <strong>
           Another Secret  Dont Type, Talk!
          </strong>
         </p>
         <p>
          Another secret of mine is that I dont type, I talk.
         </p>
         <p>
          Speech recognition software is NOT just for doctors! If you want to push your productivity through the roof, and increase your reach with blog commenting, youll definitely want to check this out.
         </p>
         <p>
          Now newer computers have built in voice
          <em>
           recognition software
          </em>
          , (you know where you talk and text populates automatically?), but if you have an older model, it may not be included. So check your Programs folder or Apps to see if this hidden gem is on your computer.
         </p>
         <p>
          Newer Macs have it built in where you tap the Function Key (fn) twice in order to activate this. A little microphone icon pops up, and if your curser is in a text editor, as you begin talking, the speech starts to appear quite magically.
         </p>
         <p>
          Let me go ahead and demonstrate.
         </p>
         <p>
          Here I have a text editor open. Im going to tap function key twice and start to speak.
         </p>
         <p>
          Hey how are you- Im doing great.
         </p>
         <p>
          How about going out later for a bite to eat, you can choose the restaurant.:-)
         </p>
         <p>
          Not one bit of editing needed this is just phenomenal. I save so much time speaking instead of typing. So I want to encourage you to use this.
         </p>
         <p>
          Now I started with a software that I got on Amazon called
          <a href="http://carolsentme.com/dragon-naturally-speaking" onclick="_gaq.push(['_trackEvent', 'outbound-article', 'http://carolsentme.com/dragon-naturally-speaking', 'Dragon Naturally Speaking']);" target="_blank">
           Dragon Naturally Speaking
          </a>
          (Its for PC or Mac).
         </p>
         <p>
          Training the software to be accustomed to your voice is necessary, but if youre willing to take a little bit of time to do this, you will reap the rewards of being able to speak any text that you otherwise would have had to type.It was well worth the investment of my time because now I type very little if at all.
         </p>
         <p>
          <strong>
           Keeping Your Sanity  Protect Your Comments
          </strong>
         </p>
         <p>
          Keeping a list of sites you like to visit is a smart way to keep organized when youre starting to make your commenting rounds.
         </p>
         <p>
          Weve all had it happen  that frustrating experience of a technical glitch causing our comment to disappear. Ive been ready to pull my hair out after spending energy and time crafting a thoughtful response  only to see it erased, and have nothing to show for my hard work.
         </p>
         <p style="text-align: justify;">
          <img alt="How to Save Time Commenting Online (and Keep Your Sanity)" class="aligncenter wp-image-155892 size-full" height="306" src="http://carolamatocdn.carolamato.netdna-cdn.com/wp-content/uploads/2014/08/losing-comments.jpg" style="border: 1px solid #941100;" width="500"/>
         </p>
         <p>
          Well, Ive tried to use Control or Command Z (as in zebra) to undo, but that doesnt always work. There are so many variables and reasons about why this can happen, so its best to stay calm, not get frustrated and just accept that it is a possibility  and focus on preventing it, which is where my tip comes in.
         </p>
         <p>
          You can speak or dictate your comment (or type) into Notepad or the text editor of your choice. When you see a comment PUBLISHED,
          <em>
           <strong>
            not in moderation
           </strong>
          </em>
          , but actually
          <span style="text-decoration: underline;">
           live on the blog
          </span>
          , then you can go ahead and type over it or erase it.
         </p>
         <p>
          But I would go ahead and name it current-comments and save it as you go. You can edit as you go. That way if you lose something by way of a glitch, its not going to affect you, and youre not going to be frustrated because you have your comments saved.
         </p>
         <p>
          Let me help you avoid what Ive been through and please follow these tips because its really going to help.
         </p>
         <p>
          If you think you dont have time to increase your reach by adding blogs you comment on or how many people you can build a relationship with, you need to think again, because using my suggestions will really work and help you to do so.
         </p>
         <p>
          <strong>
           What Do You Do To Work Smarter?
          </strong>
         </p>
         <p>
          If you have a great tip about working smarter and faster, let me know. Do you have any commenting tips? Idlove to hear about it below.
         </p>
         <p style="color: #555555; text-align: left;">

                <img alt=":-)" class="wp-smiley" src="http://carolamatocdn.carolamato.netdna-cdn.com/wp-includes/images/smilies/simple-smile.png" style="height: 1em; max-height: 1em;"/>
                (I am dictating this right now.)
               </p>
               <p>
                The transcription was dictated completely, with a little bit of editing. Thats it.
                <img alt=":-)" class="wp-smiley" src="http://carolamatocdn.carolamato.netdna-cdn.com/wp-includes/images/smilies/simple-smile.png" style="height: 1em; max-height: 1em;"/>
                SO much quicker than typing.
               </p>
               <p>
                I used to use the software you refer to about slowing down the speed of voice or speeding it up, when I was a transcriptionist, however, now all I have to do is speak and the software does the typing. No more carpal tunnel syndrome for me!
               </p>
               <p>
                Yes the free software I mentioned is very useful and what I did was use write out short keys on two or three sticky notes around my Computer monitor until I learned those, then I would throw those out and make two or three more on my monitor until I memorized those. It was a very great system and easy to remember that way, and I built up very quickly.
               </p>
               <p>
                For example, everyone wants to have their name as a short key, so you could just use the mn and then the letter x to execute.
               </p>
               <p>
                So once you set it up, mmx would populate Harleena Singh. Three keystrokes as opposed to 14 including the space you have to hit.
                <img alt=":-)" class="wp-smiley" src="http://carolamatocdn.carolamato.netdna-cdn.com/wp-includes/images/smilies/simple-smile.png" style="height: 1em; max-height: 1em;"/>
               </p>
               <p>
                The reason I use the letter x is because very few real words end with the letter x, so its convenient to use it as a trigger to execute the short key.
               </p>
               <p>
                It is very well worth the time downloading and entering short keys and keeping a few sticky notes on your monitor each day I couldnt recommend it more.  It really does make a difference at the end of a day.
               </p>
               <p>
                Its a shame your computer doesnt have the software built-in, but its pretty inexpensive on Amazon.
               </p>
               <p>
                I bet you are fantastic typist and can fly on your keyboard. Thats great!
               </p>
               <p>
                Yeah, memory in browser extensions are great, but Im referring to huge blocks of text and sentences I use on a regular basis, not just demographic stuff used to fill in forms. Its really quite versatile.
               </p>
               <p>
                Youre a smart cookie to save your comments  guess youve experienced some frustrations too, eh? Awesome to be safe with our time and work!
               </p>
               <p>
                You are very welcome, Harleena, and hope youre already having a good start to your Saturday. Thanks so much for sharing your valuable thoughts here with me and my readers.
               </p>

             </p>

              </cite>
             </div>
             <div class="dsq-comment-body" id="dsq-comment-body-130443">
              <div class="dsq-comment-message" id="dsq-comment-message-130443">
               <p>
                Hi Angela!
               </p>
               <p>
                Thanks for the kind words  much appreciated, and Im so glad you liked it.
               </p>
               <p>
                I love TypeIt4Me  wouldnt be without it. 
               </p>
               <p>
                The laptop I have is a MacBook Pro, and I tap the fn key twice to activate the voice recognition built in software. There was a time limit with it. I want the one that kept running continuously so I paid for it.
               </p>
               <p>
                Let me see what the name is, and I will tell you
               </p>
               <p>
                Okay, you have to click on System Preferences, then Dictation &amp; Speech. You have to choose On button for Dictation. I keep the box checked for Use Enhanced Dictation (allows off-line use and continuous dictation with live back). Hope that helps  you find out what settings to make sure are selected before using the short cut on your keyboard. It probably isnt activated yet.
               </p>
               <p>
                I think editing after I used dictation, is very easy. I dont have any trouble at all finding the spots that I need to edit, but it is very seldom that I do need to actually edit the text.
               </p>
               <p>
                I remember talking to you about the free transcriptions available on YouTube, and we discussed the fact that YouTube doesnt recognize your voice very well. I think thats going to be true with any type of voice recognition software or transcription software that you attempt to use.
               </p>
               <p>
                No matter what people have told you in the past, you definitely have a unique way of enunciating and pronouncing words, Angela, you have a lovely voice, but perhaps one that is not well-suited for speech recognition.
               </p>
               <p>
                However, having said that, it would just take you longer than someone else to train the software to be accustomed to your voice  but it is definitely possible, in my opinion.:-)
               </p>
               <p>
                Im so glad you got your iPhone fixed I know you were lost without it.
               </p>
               <p>
                You are very welcome, and I want to tell you how much I appreciate your warm heart-felt comment and how much I enjoy it when you come to my site.
               </p>
               <p>
                Im about to message you on Facebook, hoping to help you with your trigger box
               </p>
               <p>
                Talk soon,
               </p>
               <p>
                 Carol
               </p>
               <p>
                P. S. Yes, I did quickly scrawl out that picture, LOL!!  you know how picky I am about making sure I have unique and original pictures, and not recycled pics that dozens and hundreds of other people also have on their site.
               </p>
               <p>
                I want to rank for all rich content on my site, including images. That hand-drawn ugly pic will do me a whole lot more good than something I could get at iStockPhoto.  This strategy is already working since I recently adopted it.
               </p>

             <p>
              Hi Carol
             </p>
             <p>
              Wonderful video; passionately conceived and professionally developed.
             </p>
             <p>
              In off-page SEO the two most effective ways are guest posting and blog commenting.
             </p>
             <p>
              They are the regular off-page SEO activies unlike directory submission. So obviously time management for quality commenting is a big challenge to comment on other blogs.
             </p>
             <p>
              Earlier the purpose of blog commenting was simply to get back links. That is why the main objective was to just get the comments published and everytime we tried to go to new blog to get another back link.
             </p>
             <p>
              But now the entire philosophy of blog commenting is changed. To give quality comment we dont have any other way to first read the post fully. It takes quite sometime and after that we should put value in our comments by putting more ideas with regard to topic of the post or to create a controversy by very positively differing with a few points of the post.
             </p>
             <p>
              Doing all this if we have to type everything without any support our irritation and losing concentration is obvious.
             </p>
             <p>
              For this purpose the resources you mentioned in the post are more than sufficient and one completely overcomes physical aspect of the challenge to comment with quality.
             </p>
             <p>
              Thanks a lot for sharing a multi-type post on such an important topic. Thank you indeed.
             </p>

             </p>

                 <p>
                  Hi Carol,
                  <br/>
                  This may sound a little crazy but getting carpal tunnel symptoms is an early warning signal to me. The way I look at it is that if I have spent so much time at the keyboard that Im in pain . . . its time to step away from the computer!
                  <img alt=":)" class="wp-smiley" src="http://carolamatocdn.carolamato.netdna-cdn.com/wp-includes/images/smilies/simple-smile.png" style="height: 1em; max-height: 1em;"/>
                 </p>
                 <p>
                  I keep a Word document that I use when Im writing comments. (I mainly use it if I suspect that my comment is going to be lengthy or potentially valuable). There have been many times when I am writing a new post and I remember a discussion that Ive had (either on my blog or someone elses). All I have to do is search that document and I can often cull text that I can use in my article. It can be a real time saver.
                 </p>
                 <p>
                  Im glad to hear that you were able to spend part of the day yesterday with your son. Theres something melancholy about Labor Day weekend. Its clearly the end of one season and the beginning of another. We took our 2-year old granddaughter to a 4H Fair yesterday. It was wonderful. They grow up so fast!

             <p>
              Smart tips Carol. Ive had enough with the comments disappearing problem
              <img alt=":)" class="wp-smiley" src="http://carolamatocdn.carolamato.netdna-cdn.com/wp-includes/images/smilies/simple-smile.png" style="height: 1em; max-height: 1em;"/>
              Ive typed 3-4 paragraphs of insightful comments, clicked submit and have got a 404 error or some silly error. Going back takes me to the empty comment form! How frustrating!
             </p>
             <p>
              Recently it has become an involuntary habit to me that I cmd+A and then cmd+c anything I type before I click on the send or submit button. This not only applies to comments, but to contact forms, emails and things like that. I always select anything that I type in boxes and then click send.
             </p>
             <p>
              For comments, I copy and paste them into my sticky notes. I have more than one tabs opened. So even if my comment is lost and if I had also lost that tab (while Im hectically working lol) I can go back and retrieve that comment from my notes and paste it back to the original comment form.
             </p>
             <p>
              Thanks for the other tips
              <img alt=":)" class="wp-smiley" src="http://carolamatocdn.carolamato.netdna-cdn.com/wp-includes/images/smilies/simple-smile.png" style="height: 1em; max-height: 1em;"/>

               <p>
                Hi Jane,
               </p>
               <p>
                Why, thank you! Yes, Ive been frustrated many times, so decided to keep a running sheet of comments. Its not inconvenient to copy and paste, only takes a few seconds, and I have the assurance that my comment is safe and sound if there are technical glitches, or if perchance my comment is stuck in spam or disappears some how
               </p>
               <p>
                Its a big relief actually.
               </p>
               <p>
                The problem with comment a, and command c, then v is that our virtual clipboard only holds one copied piece of information at a time. It should be saved somewhere because you dont always know right away if there is a problem or not.
               </p>
               <p>
                I used to just do that, but found that after I copied over the previous thing, that something went awry with it and didnt have it any more. So to make sure I dont waste any time at all, I simply type in iWriter and copy and paste to my comments or whatever Im filling in. (if its more than a line or two).
               </p>
               <p>
                Yep, thats smart to have your comments stored, Jane as it will ensure your hard work does not go to waste and that you can connect with who you intended on connecting with. This is awesome!
               </p>
               <p>
                Thanks for stopping by to share your thoughts, Jane  I appreciate it.

          <li class="comment odd alt thread-even depth-1" id="dsq-comment-130696">
           <div class="dsq-comment-header" id="dsq-comment-header-130696">
            <cite id="dsq-cite-130696">
             http://www.homenotion.com/blog
             <span id="dsq-author-user-130696">
              Elizabeth McGee
             </span>
            </cite>
           </div>
           <div class="dsq-comment-body" id="dsq-comment-body-130696">
            <div class="dsq-comment-message" id="dsq-comment-message-130696">
             <p>
              Hi Carol, Thanks for those great tips!
             </p>
             <p>
              Ive tried using the voice software on my computer before and found it a little difficult to use, but I love the concept so Im definitely going to try using Shortkeys Lite.
             </p>
             <p>
              One trick that I use and love that has helped me with comments is to open all the sites I comment on at once.  Its an easy set up so if you dont mind Ill show you here:
             </p>
             <p>
              Open a notepad file and add the following:
             </p>
             <p>
              @echo off
              <br/>
              start google http://www.site1.com
              <br/>
              start google http://www.site2.com
              <br/>
              start google http://www.site3.com
             </p>
             <p>
              Add as many sites as you think your browser can hold, then save the file as a .bat file to your desktop.
             </p>
             <p>
              Then open your browser, (I use Chrome, but it should work for any browser) and click on the notepad file. Your sites should all load up.
             </p>
             <p>
              It works great for when Im ready to do comments once every few days.
             </p>
             <p>
              Thanks for the awesome post.
             </p>
             <p>
              Blessings,
              <br/>
              Liz
             </p>
            </div>
           </div>

           <div class="dsq-comment-body" id="dsq-comment-body-130766">
            <div class="dsq-comment-message" id="dsq-comment-message-130766">
             <p>
              Hey Carol,
             </p>
             <p>
              This is the marks of a true entrepreneur!
             </p>
             <p>
              Were always trying to find something that can do a lot of work for us and take less time to do it! Software like this can be of great help if youre someone like us who tend to comment on a lot of blogs
             </p>
             <p>
              I have been through the experience of writing a long thoughtful comment resulting in me losing it. I hate it when that happens, but sometimes that life.
             </p>
             <p>
              But you know what Ive been doing? After I write a comment I made the habit of copying it, just in case I lose it. If I do lose it after submission, then I can paste it back into the comment section from the clipboard. It may be an extra step but it works for me.
             </p>
             <p>
              Besides that, I usually write another comment and usually it comes out better than the previous one LOL But the software that you mentioned can definitely be very useful to save a lot of time so that you can get much more done!
             </p>
             <p>
              Thanks for sharing and I hope youre having a great week!
             </p>

             <div class="dsq-comment-header" id="dsq-comment-header-130771">

               http://www.carolamato.com/

             <div class="dsq-comment-body" id="dsq-comment-body-130771">
              <div class="dsq-comment-message" id="dsq-comment-message-130771">
               <p>
                Hi Sherman!
               </p>
               <p>
                I was so happy to see a comment from you  you made my day!
                <img alt=":-)" class="wp-smiley" src="http://carolamatocdn.carolamato.netdna-cdn.com/wp-includes/images/smilies/simple-smile.png" style="height: 1em; max-height: 1em;"/>
               </p>
               <p>
                Ya know, I used to use the copy/paste method, but a lot of times, my comment went to moderation for some reason. Then, sometimes it showed up, and sometimes it didnt. I was not willing to do the work once and lose it, so I type in a text pad and copy and paste one time, and just save them.
               </p>
               <p>
                One time, a friend wrote a guest post on a big name blog, and I commented over there. My comment went to moderation. Well, it didnt show and didnt show.
               </p>
               <p>
                Come to find out, it fell into the black hole of cyberspace, so had to search for it on my saved comment text file (always open, and all I had to do was type control f for find, and type in the persons name) and it came right up for me to copy and paste in.
               </p>
               <p>
                To me, thats priceless.
               </p>
               <p>
                We hear so much about building relationships, but if I get sick and tired of typing, it doesnt matter how much I want to connect with that person, Im burned out and dont feel like making the effort.
               </p>
               <p>
                With these tools, I never feel like that. Truly.
               </p>
               <p>
                Im glad you see the usefulness of them, Sherman, and let me know if you decide to give them a try because Id be willing to help you in any way
               </p>
               <p>
                Thanks so much for coming by to comment, I appreciate it much.
                <br/>
                 Carol
